<span id="freeTextContainer9364052416071852215"><b>Genre: </b>Contemporary Romance<br/><b>Type: </b>Standalone Book 1 of 2 from Full Tilt series<br/><b>POV: </b>First Person - Dual<br/><b>Rating: </b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454233754i/17933279.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473079615i/20402946.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Kasey Dawson was the guitarist of Rapid Confession, a band on the verge of stardom. With fame, came the downward spiral of rock and roll lifestyle that was threatening everything she worked for. She started to lose who she was inside until someone helped her see that she was so much more.<br/><br/>Jonah Fletcher was an upcoming glass artisan. With a major exhibit closing in, he worked hard to make </span>
  <span id="freeText9364052416071852215" style="display:none"><b>Genre: </b>Contemporary Romance<br><b>Type: </b>Standalone Book 1 of 2 from Full Tilt series<br><b>POV: </b>First Person - Dual<br><b>Rating: </b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454233754i/17933279.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473079615i/20402946.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kasey Dawson was the guitarist of Rapid Confession, a band on the verge of stardom. With fame, came the downward spiral of rock and roll lifestyle that was threatening everything she worked for. She started to lose who she was inside until someone helped her see that she was so much more.<br><br>Jonah Fletcher was an upcoming glass artisan. With a major exhibit closing in, he worked hard to make a mark by sticking to his rigid schedule. When Kasey came barreling into his life, he saw there's something more to life than just leaving a legacy. They both needed each other to realize what the most important thing in life is and make it worth a lifetime.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1453882133i/17883711.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I wanted to read this book for quite a while and glad finally had the chance to do so because I'm a sucker for ugly crying books. This book is not exactly ugly crying for me but a crying one none the less so that made me happy haha!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>Jonah had some magic quality about him that let me feel like myself.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>Jonah was a good guy who would make it easy for anyone to fall for him. He focused on the tasks he put forth to forget what's inevitable. He built a wall because he thought it would be easier for him and everyone else. Yet, he wasn't selfish and opened up his heart to a lost soul when he found one.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473079615i/20402947.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I love Kasey as much as Jonah - which is rare for me when it comes to heroines. She willingly jumped into the relationship knowing how far it would go.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>The solidity of him calmed me more. Not his anger, that was a shield between himself and the world, but what lay beneath.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>I love how symbiotic their relationship was. They needed each other to distract them from sinking into their personal pit. But as much as I love them, my favorite character was Theo, his brother. I don't want to elaborate much but his situation made me feel protective of him.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b> <i>No more living life halfway. We had to go full tilt, just like the card players did.</i></b>
</blockquote><br><br>Full Tilt is a story of a couple finding and living for each other, appreciating their time together to make it worthwhile. It's sad but also made you appreciate a life that isn't bound by a schedule.<br><br><i><b>Note: </b><br>I have major reservation with book 2. I don’t know how I would feel with them like that. But of course, I still want to read it hmmph! Lol!</i><br><br><br><b>⚔ ☘ ⚔ . . . <div id="review_1698780071" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1698780071" />
    <a title="Astrid - The Bookish Sweet Tooth" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7420520-astrid---the-bookish-sweet-tooth"><img alt="Astrid - The Bookish Sweet Tooth" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1558713329p2/7420520.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1698780071?book_show_action=true">Oct 04, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Astrid - The Bookish Sweet Tooth" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Astrid - The Bookish Sweet Tooth" href="/user/show/7420520-astrid---the-bookish-sweet-tooth">Astrid - The Bookish Sweet Tooth</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7420520-astrid---the-bookish-sweet-tooth?shelf=favorite-hero">favorite-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7420520-astrid---the-bookish-sweet-tooth?shelf=favorite-couples">favorite-couples</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7420520-astrid---the-bookish-sweet-tooth?shelf=must-have">must-have</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7420520-astrid---the-bookish-sweet-tooth?shelf=tear-jerker">tear-jerker</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7420520-astrid---the-bookish-sweet-tooth?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7420520-astrid---the-bookish-sweet-tooth?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7420520-astrid---the-bookish-sweet-tooth?shelf=heartbreaking">heartbreaking</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7420520-astrid---the-bookish-sweet-tooth?shelf=charming-your-pants-off-hero">charming-your-pants-off-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7420520-astrid---the-bookish-sweet-tooth?shelf=sweet-heroine">sweet-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7420520-astrid---the-bookish-sweet-tooth?shelf=aawww">aawww</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1698780071" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14690858227710842598">All the feels = all the stars in the universe!<br/><br/><a href='http://coffeecookieandbooks.blogspot.com/2016/10/all-stars-in-universe-for-emma-scott.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Review @ Vanilla & Spice Books</a><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1475770822i/20764661._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>I didn't think I had it in me still but this book...GOD! This book brought out the ugly crying and it's nice to find out that I'm not dead inside. I have no words to say how much my heart aches for Kacey and Jonah.<br/><br/>Jonah is an industrial artist who lives for his work. He creates intricate beautiful things with glass. He keeps to a carefully crafted routine to make it to the deadline of the exhibit of Jonah's legacy and m</span>
  <span id="freeText14690858227710842598" style="display:none">All the feels = all the stars in the universe!<br><br><a href="http://coffeecookieandbooks.blogspot.com/2016/10/all-stars-in-universe-for-emma-scott.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Review @ Vanilla &amp; Spice Books</a><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1475770822i/20764661._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I didn't think I had it in me still but this book...GOD! This book brought out the ugly crying and it's nice to find out that I'm not dead inside. I have no words to say how much my heart aches for Kacey and Jonah.<br><br>Jonah is an industrial artist who lives for his work. He creates intricate beautiful things with glass. He keeps to a carefully crafted routine to make it to the deadline of the exhibit of Jonah's legacy and masterpiece. He doesn't let anything get in the way of his goal.<br><br>Kacey is a musician, on the brink to success...and sick and tired of the scene. Drowning her sorrow in alcohol and meaningless sex is her coping mechanism, not only with the superficial world of music business but also with the lack of love in her life. One day when she has one drink too much, wrecked one bar too many, she ends up on the couch of her limo driver.<br><br>Jonah's and Kacey's connection is instant and while there is also a budding sexual attraction in the beginning their friendship is as innocent as it can get. They love to spend time together, making each other laugh comes naturally to them. A connection like this can't be contained though and soon feelings start to grow and turn into something else, something more. Yet, Jonah needs to keep Kacey at arms' length so he can meet the deadline of the exhibit. He offers her every part of his soul except the one piece that they both crave.<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b> "I want to be able to kiss you if I feel like it, and I think you want that too. Like our first kiss at the casino. It was everything to me. Everything."<br>"It was for me too. I want to kiss you again. I want to kiss you so bad I can't breathe. I want to be with you every second of my life..."</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>Jonah is one of the most beautiful souls I've read in any book ever. He is kind, sweet, patient, lovable in every way. He has come to terms with the fact that he will never experience being in love and his courage in the face of his condition is nothing short of amazing. With Kacey he has found his perfect match. She is his light, sweet, funny and with the same kind of courage. She teaches Jonah that focusing on the journey gives you more happiness than living only for the goal. He teaches Kacey that his love is unconditional and all encompassing. Their love is pure, life changing even. Together they create magic.<br><br>This was in no way an easy read for me. While the story was peppered with humor and light moments there was always an undertone of sadness which made me dread coming to the end. I am glad that Jonah didn't experience a miracle healing, it would have taken away from the sincerity of Jonah's and Kacey's journey. That their potentially once in a lifetime love was cut short by a cruel fate, however, hurt so much. <br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"You are not a drop in the ocean. You are the entire ocean in a drop." I looked at Kacey sitting beside me. She is not merely an ocean. She is an entire universe.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br>Emma Scott's effortless and gorgeous writing only adds to this beautiful pain. I haven't cried like this in years over a book. The secondary characters were endearing and I loved the big brother - little brother relationship between Jonah and Theo. They had a very special connection. <br><br>Even days after reading this book I'm still stunned how much fictional characters make us feel, how we can grieve for them days after closing the book. This book is easily in the top three of this year's favorites, I would even go as far as to say it's one of my top 10 ever. I can't wait to read Kacey's and Theo's way to healing and hope that Jonah's legacy will be done justice and his life will be celebrated. What I'm left with is a pile of snotty tissues and the urge to rub the spot above my heart.<br><br>I want to close this review with two quotes from an actor who left this life too soon, yet impressed me with his wisdom beyond his years:<br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Immortality is to live your life doing good things, and leaving your mark behind. The key to immortality is first living a life worth remembering."<br><br>"Because we do not know when we will die, we get to think of life as an inexhaustible well. And yet everything happens only a certain number of times, and a very small number really. How many more times will you remember a certain afternoon of your childhood, an afternoon that is so deeply a part of your being that you cannot conceive of your life without it? Perhaps four, or five times more? Perhaps not even that. How many more times will you watch the full moon rise? Perhaps twenty. And yet it all seems limitless."<br><br>- Brandon Lee</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/VanillaandSpiceBooks/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469979990i/19877036.png" width="50px” height= " class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/7420520-astrid" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469979990i/19877037.png" width="50px” height= " class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/VanSpicebooks" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469979990i/19877038.png" width="50px” height= " class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> <a href="https://www.instagram.com/vanillaandspicebooks/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1469979990i/19877039.png" width="50px” height= " class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/cordeeh/vanilla-spice-books/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1559992596" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1559992596" />
    <a title="Claire Robinson" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14026987-claire-robinson"><img alt="Claire Robinson" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1431471072p2/14026987.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1559992596?book_show_action=true">Feb 25, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Claire Robinson" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Claire Robinson" href="/user/show/14026987-claire-robinson">Claire Robinson</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/14026987-claire-robinson?shelf=shit-hot-series">shit-hot-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1559992596" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7809972795600294714">5 - <b>"You go all the way up to eleven."</b> Stars!<br/><br/><b>
  <u>Its LIVE!</u>
</b><br/><b>Amazon US</b> - <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.amazon.com/Full-Tilt-Emma-Scott-ebook/dp/B01GQFEF0S'>https://www.amazon.com/Full-Tilt-Emma...</a><br/><b>Amazon UK</b> - <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='https://www.amazon.co.uk/Full-Tilt-Emma-Scott-ebook/dp/B01GQFEF0S'>https://www.amazon.co.uk/Full-Tilt-Em...</a><br/><b>B&N</b> - <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/books/1124016208?ean=2940153092454'>http://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/books...</a><br/><br/>It’s always hard to adequately or concisely put into words my feelings after I have finished a book by Emma Scott, because each and every time she pretty much just blows me away, and leaves me an emotional mess. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466509407ra/19487322.gif' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I am pretty sure there isn’t an emotion left on the spectrum for her to wring ou</span>
  <span id="freeText7809972795600294714" style="display:none">5 - <b>"You go all the way up to eleven."</b> Stars!<br><br><b>
  <u>Its LIVE!</u>
</b><br><b>Amazon US</b> - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.amazon.com/Full-Tilt-Emma-Scott-ebook/dp/B01GQFEF0S">https://www.amazon.com/Full-Tilt-Emma...</a><br><b>Amazon UK</b> - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.amazon.co.uk/Full-Tilt-Emma-Scott-ebook/dp/B01GQFEF0S">https://www.amazon.co.uk/Full-Tilt-Em...</a><br><b>B&amp;N</b> - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/books/1124016208?ean=2940153092454">http://www.barnesandnoble.com/w/books...</a><br><br>It’s always hard to adequately or concisely put into words my feelings after I have finished a book by Emma Scott, because each and every time she pretty much just blows me away, and leaves me an emotional mess. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466509407ra/19487322.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I am pretty sure there isn’t an emotion left on the spectrum for her to wring out of me now, but with each new book, there is a new story that brings them about and always for different reasons to its predecessor.<br><br><b>"I’m a bad influence on you…"</b><br><br>There is one sentence that stood out to me from the blurb for <i>Full Tilt</i> - <br><br><b>
  <i> Jonah Fletcher is running out of time.</i>
</b><br><br>I immediately knew just from those seven words that Emma was going to rip my heart out and leave it in a bloody puddle at my feet, I have come to understand that in telling her stories it is intrinsically what she does, but in a good way. Her stories are harsh, but in a realistic way, through characters dealing with situations, conditions and just life in general, that most of us would struggle to even comprehend. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1466510743ra/19487618.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Jonah and Kacey’s relationship sort of takes a back-seat in the first half of the book, the chemistry is sizzling between them, but the author takes the time to build them up as individual characters, before moving towards being a couple. <br><br><b><i>"This is a good moment..."</i><br>"One of the best."</b><br><br>I think this is what made the second half all the more emotional for me, because you get to see who Kacey is and how much she changes in herself through the adjustments she makes in her life to understand that how she deals with her life and with being Jonah’s girlfriend is such a massive advance for her. But it’s not just that you also you see Jonah for everything he is as a man, an artist and a lover, and not just the situation that he is being defined by in the present.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466508782i/19487183._SY540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don’t want to say a huge amount about the story-line as a whole, this is Emma Scott writing, so you know it’s going to be a little different from the norm, everything that happens is for a reason it may not be apparent straight away, but everything has a clarity to it as the story progresses, I have a feeling that potentially a few things that happened in this book with what are currently secondary characters may have a bearing on the second book, but I may be wrong with that one, it’s just a couple of things stood out to me, and I am interested to see if my thoughts bear fruit when I get too read <i>All In</i> later this year. <br><br><b>"I’m more afraid of not being with you than I am of being with you."</b><br><br>The plot pacing is kept at a level that for me personally I pretty much read most of the book with the itch of anticipation niggling just under my skin, mix that with a pretty big lump in my throat, as well that when that tidal wave of emotion hits you in the latter stages of this couples story, and <i>believe</i> me it will, I just had to let it go and get it all out.<br><br><b>
  <i>She was so much. I could spend a thousand full lifetimes and never reach the end of her…</i>
</b><br><br>Emma knows how I feel about her writing, I could sit here and gush for hours about every book I have read by her, if you have read her books before you will know somewhat, what to expect with <i>Full Tilt,</i> if you haven’t I urge you to give her a try, you have nothing to lose and a whole list of awesome books to discover. <br><br><b>"I can take it, whatever happens."</b><br><br>I may need to invest in stronger tissues and a larger wine glass though! Emma Scott I bow down to your awesome mad-writing-skillz, you delivered again, and I cannot wait for the conclusion to this story.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1386600797ra/7400145.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>ARC provided by the author, the review was my absolute pleasure to offer.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1457954696i/18425325._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="7809972795600294714" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1778805194" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1778805194" />
    <a title="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books"><img alt="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1528808758p2/37314676.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1778805194?book_show_action=true">Oct 14, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" class="user" itemprop="url" name="NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}" href="/user/show/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books">NiCoLeTa E. {Addicted To Books}</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books?shelf=romance-young-adult-etc">romance-young-adult-etc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/37314676-nicoleta-e-addicted-to-books?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1778805194" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3749074219609009813"><b>
  <i>***5++ "No regrets!!!" stars***</i>
</b><br/><br/><b>
  <u>Full tilt (n) (poker):</u>
</b> <i>Playing emotionally instead of rationally; making impassioned rather than logical decisions.</i><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478459197i/21075305.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"No more living life halfway. We had to go full tilt, just like the card players did. I would hit instead of stay. Always."</i>
</b><br/><br/>I have many days since I've finished "Full Tilt" and my feelings are still over the place... The words don't come easily this time and I'm struggling to put my thoughts in the right order...<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478459197ra/21075306.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>This book wrecked me in a way</span>
  <span id="freeText3749074219609009813" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>***5++ "No regrets!!!" stars***</i>
</b><br><br><b>
  <u>Full tilt (n) (poker):</u>
</b> <i>Playing emotionally instead of rationally; making impassioned rather than logical decisions.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478459197i/21075305.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"No more living life halfway. We had to go full tilt, just like the card players did. I would hit instead of stay. Always."</i>
</b><br><br>I have many days since I've finished "Full Tilt" and my feelings are still over the place... The words don't come easily this time and I'm struggling to put my thoughts in the right order...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478459197ra/21075306.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This book wrecked me in a way, but at the same time gave me so much hope!!! <br><i>Hope that love exist in the darkest places and it can be a balm... <br>Hope that love is enough even though if it exists in only small moments!!!</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478459197ra/21075307.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“We might not have months or years, but we have moments. Thousands upon thousands of them. Let’s take each moment, seize it and wring it dry. Okay?”</i>
</b><br><br>This book was marvellous and the story grabbed my heart from the very first page till the last one and I'm pretty positive that it will stay with me forever...<br>I loved fiercely the protagonists and the secondary characters, i loved the storyline even though that it was harsh, i loved Mrs Scott's writing and the way that she handle this gentle matter....<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1448708061ra/17179335.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I loved the hope, the love, the moments that it gave me.... <br>I loved the heartbreak and the grief that it also brought to me because it was pure...<br><i>Love can hurt and love can heal!!! Even when there is no time, it can be a salvation!!!</i><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478459197ra/21075308.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><b>
  <i>“I’m with you, Kacey. I can’t not be with you.”<br>“No going back, okay? No second-guessing. If we do, we just waste time. I don’t want to waste a single moment with you. Not one.” </i>
</b><br><br><b>This was Jonah and Kacey's story...</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467820190ra/19634693.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Kacey was lost... She was surrounded by buzz, parties, many meaningless hook ups, the rock star lifestyle, but she wasn't satisfied. She was lost inside and she didn't know how to get out in the light...<br>She was still hurting of what had happened to her many years before and she was copying only with destruction....<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478459197ra/21075310.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Jonah's past was good!!! He had great parents, great friends, a loving brother, a great carreer ahead of him, but before a while, everything turned upside down in his life...<br>His life became a fight with time... He needed this time to focus on his art and to his legacy...<br>He didn't need any distractions...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478459197ra/21075311.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“Thanks for being a good guy, Jonah. There’s a shortage in the world.”</i>
</b> <i>{Kacey}</i><br><br><b>
  <i>“A legacy,” he said. “That’s all I wanted... I never thought to ask for more.”</i>
</b> <i>{Jonah}</i><br><br>But distraction came with the form of a wasted rock star and even though Jonah had to stick to his plan, he couldn't let Kacey alone... His protective insticts kicked in and everything changed for both of them....<br>A great love was born, a love full of tiny moments who changed their lives forever...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478459197ra/21075312.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Jonah was afraid to let Kacey in because he wanted to protect her from the heartbreaking that it was bound to happen... And Kacey was determined to stay there with him and chase away her fears...<br>In a hopeless future, something great was about to happen....<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478459197ra/21075313.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“And yet,” I said, gulping air, getting a hold of myself. “Here I am.”<br>“Here you are…” Jonah said, his eyes roaming my face. “Believe me, I didn’t want to let you in. But it was almost as if…”<br>“What?” I whispered.<br>“As if I didn’t have a choice,” Jonah said. “I tried to keep the circle closed and my walls up, keep to my routine…But you got in anyway.”</i>
</b><br><br>I loved so much both Kacey and Jonah...<br>They were so perfect together.... They saved each other in a lifechanging love... For both of them...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478459197ra/21075314.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>Kacey was full of life, but she was drowing fast... She needed a push from Jonah to appreciate life and embrace it...<br>Jonah needed Kacey to find out what he was missing from his life...<br>Jonah was such a great guy... I have no words to explain how wonderfull, selfless and awesome guy he was!!! And Kacey was his universe...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1419963476ra/13150968.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>"You are a universe, Kacey.<br>I kept waiting to find the end of your love and beauty, the end of your generous heart. I never did. I never will. I don’t know how or why you chose me to love, and you did choose. You could’ve walked away and saved yourself. Instead, you chose to stay, and so saved me. That’s my legacy: I loved you and was loved by you."</i>
</b> <i>{Jonah}</i><br><br><b>
  <i>“I love you,” I said. “You’re the best thing to ever happen to me. I wouldn’t give back one second of our time together. Not one.”<br>“Kace…” he breathed...<br> “My heart’s breaking,” I said. “And I’m so happy. You make me so happy. Your love’s made me strong. You’ve made me a better person…” <br>“Being loved by you, Jonah…it’s the greatest honor of my life.”</i>
</b> <i>{Kacey}</i><br><br>I cried so damn much in this book, but i wouldn't change anything in it!!!<br>Yes, many times i was wondering if things should be done this way but i think that this was the right path... even though the grief was clutching my heart and didn't let me go... <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1468859056ra/19753323.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>I still hurt for the turn of the events even though that i was being prepared!!! <br>You just can't be prepared for something like that... In real world and in the fictional...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478459197ra/21075315.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“You’re so brave,” I said. “You’re the bravest person I know.”<br>“Not me,” she said. “Brave or scared shitless, I don’t have a choice but to love you.” </i>
</b><br><br>I also liked to tell you that except Jonah and Kacey were other wonderful people in here....<br>The Fletchers, Oscar and Dena with her wonderful Rumi's quotes and of course Theo....<br>The overprotecting, kind and wonderful Theo.... <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478459197ra/21075316.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br>A guy that touched my heart with all this love and devotion that he had for his brother.... <br>But i will talk about him later....<br><br>Finally, i will have to add that i like every form of art and here, we were having lots of different kinds.... Music, tattoos and glass blowing...<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478459197i/21075317._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Damn, Jonah's glass blowing was magnificent and it magnitized me...<br>I wish i would be able to see his legacy with my own two eyes!!!!<br><br>I don't think that i will get over this ending and Jonah will always stay with me, so I'm really afraid of what will happen next...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472298096ra/20177336.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>How can you get over a guy like Jonah, ugh???</i><br><br><b>
  <i>"I felt him in every pore, every breath and beat of our hearts. I’d never experienced anything like this in my life. He was a universe. My love for him was just as boundless.<br>Tears filled our eyes as our bodies rolled and slid, driving toward a bittersweet crescendo of pleasure. Tears for love. For loss. For the weeks he had, and the years he didn’t. For the joy and laughter, the heartache and grief. For this lonely man and the lost woman he’d rescued. For us, and the rapidly approaching time in which there would be only me..."</i>
</b><br><br>Thank you Emma Scott for this wonderful story!!!<br>It got straight into my heart!!!! <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1464705240ra/19266710.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>“Lovers don’t finally meet somewhere. They are in each other all along,”</b> <i>-Rumi</i><br><br><i>***ARC generously provided via NetGalley for the exchange of an honest review***</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="3749074219609009813" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer12420627193625881376">5 infinite stars!! <br/><br/>I thought I knew what I was getting with this book but I was so wrong it went beyond my expectations. So amazingly beautiful but then, I shouldn't be surprised I have loved Emma Scott's stories ever since I read my first book by her "love beyond words". <br/><br/>"Full tilt" is the story of kacey and Jonah, they meet under really difficult circumstances. Jonah, is terminally ill, his working hard so that he can leave his legacy and every moment is so precious for him. You can say their </span>
  <span id="freeText12420627193625881376" style="display:none">5 infinite stars!! <br><br>I thought I knew what I was getting with this book but I was so wrong it went beyond my expectations. So amazingly beautiful but then, I shouldn't be surprised I have loved Emma Scott's stories ever since I read my first book by her "love beyond words". <br><br>"Full tilt" is the story of kacey and Jonah, they meet under really difficult circumstances. Jonah, is terminally ill, his working hard so that he can leave his legacy and every moment is so precious for him. You can say their love affair has no beginning but a middle with a heart wrenching end.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478856091ra/21120740.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Both these characters were the heart and soul of this book, from the moment they meet you feel their connection even though they tried to fight it. Kacey, finding her life out of control, partying and drinking with her band. Meeting Jonah, saves her, he makes her see her worth, her talent. Jonah, sweet handsome Jonah, so caring trying hard to fight his feelings for kacey not wanting to give her anymore pain. But how do they fight it?! when they have moments and not forevers. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478854584i/21120518.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I truly don't know what's better knowing that their time together was so short or not knowing at all. Regardless it was bittersweet seeing them together, how effortless their love grew. Even though their time was short the intensity of their feelings made it so heart wrenching beautiful. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1478854584ra/21120519.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Apart from the romantic part of this book, the family love and friends love was so wonderful as well. Especially the bond between Jonah, and his brother Theodore, who was so serious but loved him fiercely. I know that teddy would of given his life for Jonah, if given the chance that's how deep I felt they loved each other. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478854584i/21120520.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478854585i/21120521.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm so glad I finally read this book the tears I cried, the emotions I went through with this story, I'll treasure always. The wonderful message it has, it makes you think how precious life is, how we have to enjoy every moment as much as possible with the ones we love.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1457671161ra/18386153.gif" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>At the end I felt raw heartbroken but I know the second book brings healing and the HEA that I crave. &lt;3<br><br></span>

<div id="review_3070872869" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/3070872869" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3070872869?book_show_action=true">Dec 03, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mali Mor ❤️ The Romantic Blogger" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mali Mor ❤️ The Romantic Blogger" href="/user/show/88472183-mali-mor-the-romantic-blogger">Mali Mor ❤️ The Romantic Blogger</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3070872869" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6901976791473728102"><a href='https://ibb.co/NjgyXv8' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1575362152ra/28548645.gif' alt='ez-gif-com-video-to-gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Casey, a guitarist in a rock band, was looking for love and acceptance her hole life after her father threw her out at the age of 17. 💣<br/>She's impulsive and reckless, drinks too much, celebrates too much and has too many one night stands to actually find a true love. 💔<br/><br/>After another crazy night of celebrations and alcohol, she wakes up and finds herself on a couch at Jonah's house, a limo driver hired for the band - and a glass artist. 💘<br/>Jonah is one of those heroes who you just know has a golde</span>
  <span id="freeText6901976791473728102" style="display:none"><a href="https://ibb.co/NjgyXv8" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1575362152ra/28548645.gif" alt="ez-gif-com-video-to-gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Casey, a guitarist in a rock band, was looking for love and acceptance her hole life after her father threw her out at the age of 17. 💣<br>She's impulsive and reckless, drinks too much, celebrates too much and has too many one night stands to actually find a true love. 💔<br><br>After another crazy night of celebrations and alcohol, she wakes up and finds herself on a couch at Jonah's house, a limo driver hired for the band - and a glass artist. 💘<br>Jonah is one of those heroes who you just know has a golden heart and will leave you wanting for more. 😍<br><br>📚 “𝑾𝒆 𝒅𝒐 𝒏𝒐𝒕 𝒓𝒆𝒎𝒆𝒎𝒃𝒆𝒓 𝒅𝒂𝒚𝒔, 𝒘𝒆 𝒓𝒆𝒎𝒆𝒎𝒃𝒆𝒓 𝒎𝒐𝒎𝒆𝒏𝒕𝒔.” 📚<br> <br>Although they are complete opposites, Casey and Jonah develop a strong friendship that becomes a greater than life love story. 💞<br>But Jonah has a secret... one that makes him push people away... <br>one that can destroy both of them. 💥<br><br>The only one who doesn't give up on him is his little brother, Theo. A tough tattoo artist with a huge heart - they are so different, but the love between the two is so special that it totally made me jealous of their bond! 😍<br><br>📚 “𝑾𝒆 𝒎𝒂𝒚 𝒏𝒐𝒕 𝒉𝒂𝒗𝒆 𝒎𝒐𝒏𝒕𝒉𝒔 𝒐𝒓 𝒚𝒆𝒂𝒓𝒔, 𝒃𝒖𝒕 𝒘𝒆 𝒉𝒂𝒗𝒆 𝒎𝒐𝒎𝒆𝒏𝒕𝒔. 𝑻𝒉𝒐𝒖𝒔𝒂𝒏𝒅𝒔 𝒖𝒑𝒐𝒏 𝒕𝒉𝒐𝒖𝒔𝒂𝒏𝒅𝒔 𝒐𝒇 𝒕𝒉𝒆𝒎. 𝑳𝒆𝒕’𝒔 𝒕𝒂𝒌𝒆 𝒆𝒂𝒄𝒉 𝒎𝒐𝒎𝒆𝒏𝒕, 𝒔𝒆𝒊𝒛𝒆 𝒊𝒕 𝒂𝒏𝒅 𝒘𝒓𝒊𝒏𝒈 𝒊𝒕 𝒅𝒓𝒚. 𝑶𝒌𝒂𝒚?” 📚<br> <br>I thought I was going to read a romantic book about a rock star with a "normal" guy- instead, my heart was torn to a million pieces. 💔 <br>Luckily, the second book corrected it and reminded me that even in the most difficult moments, love will heal everything! 😍<br><br>For a whole weekend, I lived through these three characters... I fell in love with Jonah, Casey and Theo - and their heartbreaking (but hopeful) story. 🙏<br><br>📚 "...𝑰𝒏𝒔𝒕𝒆𝒂𝒅 𝒐𝒇 𝒇𝒆𝒆𝒍𝒊𝒏𝒈 𝒃𝒂𝒅 𝒕𝒉𝒂𝒕 𝒊𝒕 𝒆𝒏𝒅𝒆𝒅, 𝑰'𝒎 𝒋𝒖𝒔𝒕 𝒉𝒂𝒑𝒑𝒚 𝒊𝒕 𝒉𝒂𝒑𝒑𝒆𝒏𝒆𝒅." 📚<br> <br>Even so, I must point out that I anticipated (and rather quickly) everything that was about to happen - and even though it kind of bothered me, I still managed to enjoy the book and fall completely in love... ❤<br><br>This duet will make your heart beet faster, hurt your stomach and evokes a lot of emotion even after you finish reading. It reminded me to appreciate the little moments we take for granted... 💔<br>That's why when I finished, I set a date night with my sisters, Just because I wanted a hug. 😉👑<br><br> 📖 ᖴOᒪᒪOᗯ ᗰE Oᑎ IᑎᔕTᗩGᖇᗩᗰ: 🎉 <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://www.instagram.com/the_romantic_blogger/">https://www.instagram.com/the_romanti...</a></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17723129356289723392">I can honestly say, I read the reviews, I knew what to expect, hence probably why I was crying as I read the instant chemistry, the instant connection, between two amazing characters. But dang it, I held the hope out, I put it high up there that maybe just maybe....... Jonah & Kacey are two souls that are literally put on this earth for each other. This book was hard to read. It wasn't just because of the sadness, the heartbreaking tragedy but because I was in an airport for the first 85% of thi</span>
  <span id="freeText17723129356289723392" style="display:none">I can honestly say, I read the reviews, I knew what to expect, hence probably why I was crying as I read the instant chemistry, the instant connection, between two amazing characters. But dang it, I held the hope out, I put it high up there that maybe just maybe....... Jonah &amp; Kacey are two souls that are literally put on this earth for each other. This book was hard to read. It wasn't just because of the sadness, the heartbreaking tragedy but because I was in an airport for the first 85% of this book on a long layover. So I sat there bawling my eyes out, yep I was that person everyone was thinking was leaving her loved ones. Funny thing was, they were with, scattered about getting away from me but with that said, this book is that good. I didn't care where I was, the authors writing brought out every fricken emotion within me. It's one of those beautiful ones that no matter the depth of how sad it is, it's so much more beautiful❤️❤️❤️</span>

<div id="review_1723821061" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1723821061" />
    <a title="KAS" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/20691061-kas"><img alt="KAS" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1472348331p2/20691061.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1723821061?book_show_action=true">Aug 09, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="KAS" class="user" itemprop="url" name="KAS" href="/user/show/20691061-kas">KAS</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/20691061-kas?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1723821061" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10085007693489330763">Whew!!! ....... Been trying for hours to get my act together to write this review after reading this devastatingly beautiful love story. I have read many books that emotionally wiped me out, but my goodness!!! This was an awesome read and one I will never forget! For those of you who desire a book and its characters to tug deeply and steal a piece of your heart, this is definitely for you. One needs to be very careful how they describe what they have just read so as to not give away any spoilers</span>
  <span id="freeText10085007693489330763" style="display:none">Whew!!! ....... Been trying for hours to get my act together to write this review after reading this devastatingly beautiful love story. I have read many books that emotionally wiped me out, but my goodness!!! This was an awesome read and one I will never forget! For those of you who desire a book and its characters to tug deeply and steal a piece of your heart, this is definitely for you. One needs to be very careful how they describe what they have just read so as to not give away any spoilers, but I will say "Caution: tissues recommended." Here is a my brief synopsis before Kacey and Jonah met and went "Full Tilt"!<br /><br />Kacey Dawson, age 22, should be ecstatic. She has the world by the tail. Her band, Rapid Confession, is on tour in Vegas and she is quickly becoming a rock star goddess. Instead of joy, all she feels is loneliness and aches for something she's never felt...... loved, specifically loved by her parents. No matter what she does or doesn't do, it never pleases them. Her specialty is rritating and enraging her father. At age seventeen, he kicked her out of the house and she was forced to live on the streets. Now, four years later, she still isn't welcomed back home, nor will her father speak to her. But hey, at least she is adored by her screaming fans. Life for Kacey is reduced to guzzling vodka from a water bottle, partying 24/7 and totally spirally out of control.<br /><br />Jonah Fletcher, age 26, works at night as a limo driver in Las Vegas and by day works as a glass artist. He desperately needs his limo job, but Kacey nearly gets him fired one night after performing at a rock concert. Her world collides with his, and at age 22 and 26, their lives FINALLY begin.<br /><br />This is my first book by Emma Scott and it sure won't be my last. She had me sucked in by the end of the first paragraph of the prologue. Her writing skills are superb!<br /><br />*I received a copy of this book, via Netgalley, in exchange for an honest review*</span>
  <a data-text-id="10085007693489330763" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1844644976" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1844644976" />
    <a title="Talia (Red Hot Ink)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/25505540-talia-red-hot-ink"><img alt="Talia (Red Hot Ink)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1472896405p2/25505540.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1844644976?book_show_action=true">Jan 03, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Talia (Red Hot Ink)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Talia (Red Hot Ink)" href="/user/show/25505540-talia-red-hot-ink">Talia (Red Hot Ink)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25505540-talia-red-hot-ink?shelf=heart-breaking">heart-breaking</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25505540-talia-red-hot-ink?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25505540-talia-red-hot-ink?shelf=book-boyfriends">book-boyfriends</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25505540-talia-red-hot-ink?shelf=sweet-guy">sweet-guy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/25505540-talia-red-hot-ink?shelf=perfectly-imperfect-hero">perfectly-imperfect-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer1844644976&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1844644976" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6987819391605365052"><b>5 Thousands of moments stars</b><br/><br/><i>ARC provided by Netgalley in exchange for an honest review</i><br/><br/>THERE ARE PROBABLY GOING TO BE SPOILERS, SO DO NOT READ IF YOU'RE GOING TO READ THIS BOOK. I'M SERIOUS. A SINGLE SPOILER COULD RUIN YOUR WHOLE READING EXPERIENCE.<br/><br/><br/><br/><br/><br/>Do you know what "The Fault of Our Stars" and "Me Before You" have in common besides the obvious? That I haven't read them. I wouldn't touch them with a ten foot pole because reading is my escape from reality. Having my heart ripped out of my chest is </span>
  <span id="freeText6987819391605365052" style="display:none"><b>5 Thousands of moments stars</b><br><br><i>ARC provided by Netgalley in exchange for an honest review</i><br><br>THERE ARE PROBABLY GOING TO BE SPOILERS, SO DO NOT READ IF YOU'RE GOING TO READ THIS BOOK. I'M SERIOUS. A SINGLE SPOILER COULD RUIN YOUR WHOLE READING EXPERIENCE.<br><br><br><br><br><br>Do you know what "The Fault of Our Stars" and "Me Before You" have in common besides the obvious? That I haven't read them. I wouldn't touch them with a ten foot pole because reading is my escape from reality. Having my heart ripped out of my chest is not my idea of fun.<br>I don't do emotional reads. It's not my thing.<br><br>It's not what I'm used to. In PRN if someone dies chances are they're going to resuscitare in less than 3 chapters. In contemporary romances we have cases à la Jake Weston, or Warren McPhearson. I guess one of the reasons it hit me so hard and so suddenly in the end it was because I wasn't expecting it. Now you're probably thinking: "What special brand of stupid must you be not to expect it when it's clear from page one?" My answer is: "The brand that is used to HEA, kittens and rainbows, even when there's a slew of bullets Swiss-cheesing a character's heart." I was so sure something would happen and save him. Namely Theo dying somehow and donating all his compatible organs to his brother. I was hoping for it to happen, and I don't care if that makes me a bad person. Even after I read the word "funeral" I was sure it was Theo's and that the author would soon say something like "Jonah walked to his brother's grave." When that didn't happen... that's when I lost it.<br><br>It was the ineluctability of it all that torn me. He didn't do anything bad. It was no ones' fault. It was just the way his life went. And although it was incredible the way he lived his last months, the love he and Kacey shared... it still left me bereft and grieving. <br><br>Jonah's character was so remarkable, which made his death so much more unbearable. He's this sweet, talented, brave young man who at times made me even forget of his condition because until the last third of the book he was somewhat normal. I loved his POVs, how he always tried to wring life out of every moment, but without desperation. He was so quiet in his beauty and strength.<br><br><i>
  <b>I watched the firelight cast a glow over the faces of the people I loved best. I captured the moments in mental snapshots.<br>Oscar's laughing face, firelight catching Dena's earring, Holly's squeak of alarm when her marshmallow caught fire, Theo holding a hot dog straight up and turning his head sideways to bite it. And Kacey leaning her chin on the heel of her hand, glancing sideways at me, leaning toward me...<br>I committed these moments to memories with the hope I might take them with me wherever I went next.</b>
</i><br><br>Kacey was a surprise. At first I was wary of her, but the changes in her life she did for him and for herself, the mere fact that she was strong enough to stick around until the end... I wanted to hug her so much. I wanted to take away her pain because, especially in the second part, Scott truly managed to make their relationship bloom and blossom into this rare, perfect flower. And maybe its perfection was partly due to the desperation lacing their time together, to that "live in the moment" attitude they were forced to adopt. Whatever the reason, Kacey's evolution was almost a rebirth.<br><br>Their relationship was such a natural progression. It was slow at first, since Jonah pushed her away, not wanting her to get to attached to someone with an expiration date. But as time passed, it was clear they were inevitable. When they finally jumped into it, it felt right, it felt perfect, like it was the obvious next-step.<br><br><i>
  <b>Jonah held me as I floated on my back, my head in the curve of his shoulder, and I had the fleeting wish that we </b>
</i>could live here. Not in San Diego but in this day, these moments, over and over again, forever. <br><br>The writing style was flawless. It adorned my heart with the most beautiful, warming feelings, only to shatter it like glass in the end. The characters felt real, alive, pulsing; and even though this book crushed me and left me gasping through the tears, I'm happy it happened.<br><br>Kacey said: "I had known Jonah Fletcher. I had been loved by him, and it was a privilege I would carry with me for the rest of my life".<br><br>That's how I feel: honored to have read such a wonderful book. Honored to have read Jonah's story, to have known him through Scott's words.<br><br>Where to find me:<br><br><a href="https://twitter.com/Talia_RedHotInk" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477260342i/20933160._SY540_.png" alt="716251" width="48" height="48" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="https://www.facebook.com/Red-Hot-Ink-317503885280425/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1477260342i/20933161.png" alt="101920-simple-red-glossy-icon-social-media-logos-facebook-logo" width="52" height="52" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="https://redhotink.wordpress.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <br>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1475842301i/20773010.gif" width="150" height="150" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1779913508?book_show_action=true">Oct 09, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chantal ❤️" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chantal ❤️" href="/user/show/39644830-chantal">Chantal ❤️</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1779913508" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14233322547657286037"><b>5 REVISED STARS</b><br/><br/>After reading the second book all the issues I had previous had with this book has been removed. <br/><br/>THIS BOOK ROCKED! I F*CKING LOVED EVERY DYSFUNCTIONAL WORD OF IT!!! <br/>Keeping the first review anyways but I changed my mind about the rating after the EPIC book two here!<br/><br/>Hope you give it a try guys! <br/>You won't regret it! <br/><br/><b>4 HEARTBROKEN STARS<br/><br/>"LOVE HIM LIKE YOU LOVED ME. LOVE HIM MORE.” His eyes closed. “I’m so happy...Make someone else…as happy as I am right now. Okay? Promise.”</b><br/><br/>Yes, it's t</span>
  <span id="freeText14233322547657286037" style="display:none"><b>5 REVISED STARS</b><br><br>After reading the second book all the issues I had previous had with this book has been removed. <br><br>THIS BOOK ROCKED! I F*CKING LOVED EVERY DYSFUNCTIONAL WORD OF IT!!! <br>Keeping the first review anyways but I changed my mind about the rating after the EPIC book two here!<br><br>Hope you give it a try guys! <br>You won't regret it! <br><br><b>4 HEARTBROKEN STARS<br><br>"LOVE HIM LIKE YOU LOVED ME. LOVE HIM MORE.” His eyes closed. “I’m so happy...Make someone else…as happy as I am right now. Okay? Promise.”</b><br><br>Yes, it's that type of book! You know that book that makes you hug your kids a little bit harder and kiss your lover a little bit longer. <br>It makes you grateful for all the blessings in your life. <br>Tomorrow is Thanksgiving in Canada and this book sets the tone for my deep appreciation of all my HEALTHY FAMILY members. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1476054125i/20796642._SX540_.jpg" width="450" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story is about Kacey a young lady searching in vain for love, acceptance, and a path to happiness. She is a reckless rock star/musician, who is looking for love in all the wrong place with all the wrong people. She has been kicked out of her house by her dad at 17 and left to live in a shelter. She finds a friend and joins a band with her. She drinks too much, smokes too much, and has too many one night stands.<br><br>Kacey is the type of heroine that I usually avoid as they have the power to be unpredictable when it comes to loyalty. I am happy to say that this was not the case here. She is 100% true blue when it comes to the hero Jonah.<br><br><br>Now Jonah I ADORE. HE IS ONE TRULY BEAUTIFUL SOUL. He has been dealt a cold hand but he is trying to adjust to altered reality. He is her limo driver and one night they share a connection that was to be their salvation and their motivation for the future. They are both reluctant hero and heroine. Two perfectly damaged souls, that are beautiful together. <br><br>With all their struggles and trials I felt they deserved their happiness, and when it came to the end I was left DEVASTATED! <br><b>We are talking big ugly cry! With hiccups!</b><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1463981007ra/19180782.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Now why did I give it only 4 stars because this book is clearly a 5 star read here! If it had been based only on the amount of emotional involvement it would be 5++ stars. <br>However, two reason it's not is that I was left with an ending THAT JUST ENDS! <br>No closures at all and we have to read another book! Also there is small matter of the hero,<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[he does dies at the end! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> I am being honest here when I say I can't give 5 stars when the author does that. Usually it's a 2 or 2.5 star read because half the book is irrelevant now. <br><br>This is a story that will stay with me for days and maybe even longer. The way I feel right now, I am a complete emotional mess...I am exhausted. <br>This book is worth it!<b> <br>It is worth a read!</b><br>This book should not have worked for me at all here but it did...It really truly did.<br><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380428273ra/856826.gif" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Safety: perfectly safe we get no prior sexual acts from either the hero and the heroine. They are both sexually experienced and faithful to each other. Get together, stay together, no OM/OW drama And condoms are always used.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('ncW3B9J0MOtykMeMI6fMVsDlcNuGXRzBZStQ9XK7CDbGKbe0rGLv5gcIm/jjRvO1asSZyFUejTrdhlMjvM1yAA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

Und je näher sie ihm kommt, desto größer wird die Gefahr, in die sie sich begibt … \nEin gefühlsintensiver, mitreißender, romantischer Liebesroman, der dich nicht mehr loslassen wird. \n\nWenn wir aufeinandertreffen, sprühen keine Funken. Wenn wir aufeinandertreffen, gehen wir in Flammen auf.\nSein Name lautete Ches. Das war alles, was ich wusste. Keine Vergangenheit und keine Identität. Alles an ihm strahlte Gefahr aus, doch ich schaffte es einfach nicht, mich von ihm fernzuhalten. Ich war Metall und er der Magnet, welcher mich anzog. Doch nicht nur mich zog er an; auch Dunkelheit und Ärger und Geheimnisse begleiteten ihn wie Motten das Licht. Ich war vielleicht gebrochen, aber wenn er mich für schwach hielt, machte er einen Fehler. Ich würde jedes seiner Geheimnisse lüften. Und wenn ich brennen musste, um seine Dunkelheit zu vertreiben, würde ich jede Sekunde im Feuer genießen.\n\nTami Fischer ist Buchhändlerin und Buch-Bloggerin. Sie liebt romantische Geschichten und hat mit »Burning Bridges« ihre erste eigene gefühlvolle und spannende Romance geschrieben. Es handelt sich um Teil 1 einer Reihe, die in den USA an der Fletcher University spielt und sich rund um Ellas Clique dreht. In den Folgebänden der Fletcher-University-Reihe wird jeweils eine Freundin von Ella im Mittelpunkt stehen. Entdecke doch gleich Teil 2 der Reihe, »Sinking Ships«, in dem Carla für ihre Liebe zu Mitchell ihre größte Angst überwinden muss … \nWeitere Bände werden folgen. <span id="freeTextContainer16634866556443691504">Emma Scott is a <i>USA Today</i> and <i>Wall St. Journal </i> bestselling author whose books have been translated in five languages and featured in Buzzfeed, Huffington Post, New York Daily News and USA Today’s Happy Ever After. Her first MM romance, Someday, Someday won the Utopia Con Award for LGBTQ Book of the Year. Emma writes emotional, character-driven romances in which art and love intertwine to heal, an</span>
  <span id="freeText16634866556443691504" style="display:none">Emma Scott is a <i>USA Today</i> and <i>Wall St. Journal </i> bestselling author whose books have been translated in five languages and featured in Buzzfeed, Huffington Post, New York Daily News and USA Today’s Happy Ever After. Her first MM romance, Someday, Someday won the Utopia Con Award for LGBTQ Book of the Year. Emma writes emotional, character-driven romances in which art and love intertwine to heal, and in which love always wins.
